     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Maryland">Maryland</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="City_of_Salisbury.2C_Maryland">City of Salisbury, Maryland</span></h5> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.wicomicocounty.org/">Wicomico County</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ci.salisbury.md.us/publicworks/index.htm">City of Salisbury</a> The joint City of Salisbury/Wicomico County GIS group maintains detailed and accurate GIS data that is, through personal conversation with both City and County GIS coordinators, public domain. Efforts are being made to make this data publicly available through venues such as Open Street Map and internally hosted public web maps. Uploaded data includes the most recent, up-to-date City administrative boundary, building footprints, and more extensive coverage of hydrology data for the majority of the Wicomico County/City of Salisbury metrocore area. </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Prince_George.27s_County.2C_Maryland"><b>Prince George's County, Maryland</b></span></h5> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.princegeorgescountymd.gov/">Prince George's County</a> maintains an <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gisdata.pgplanning.org/opendata/">OpenData portal for GIS</a> which <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.pgplanning.org/Resources/Tools_On-line/GIS_and_Mapping_Tools.htm">launched July 1, 2015</a> which contains 200+ datasets including: building shapefiles, points of interest by category type, hydro structures, contour lines, and other features for the entire county in Maryland. The website does not explicitly state public domain, but per their <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.pgplanning.org/Assets/Planning/Information+Management/GIS-ODI.pdf">GIS Open Data Initiative PDF</a> "The data, which is available at no cost, includes planimetric, property, zoning, terrain, administrative, census, environmental, historic, infrastructure, and park facility datasets." The website also notes: </p> 
     <ul>
      <li> <i>Data Use Restrictions</i>: Unless otherwise noted, the information provided can be copied, modified, distributed, analyzed, and used for commercial purposes without requesting permission. The Planning Department makes no warranties about the data and disclaims liability for all uses of the data to the fullest extent permitted by applicable law.</li>
     </ul> 
     <ul>
      <li> <i>Attribution request, but not required</i>: While not required, the Planning Department requests attribution. The example attribution provided: Data retrieved from Planning Department GIS Open Data http://www.pgplanning.org</li>
     </ul> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Massachusetts">Massachusetts</span></h4> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.mass.gov/mgis/download.htm">MassGIS</a> main download page. The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://wiki.openstreetmap.org/index.php/Import/Catalogue">import Catalog</a> lists this as imported with a <b>massgis_import_*</b> tag. Which layers were imported? See <a href="/wiki/MassGIS" title="MassGIS">MassGIS</a> for the trail of breadcrumbs. Several layers imported, including roads, points of interest, building outines in Boston, and OpenSpace (2009-01-04), by CRSchmidt. </p>
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.mass.gov/mgis/ldtrails.htm">Long distance trails</a> and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.mass.gov/mgis/biketrails.htm">Bike Trails</a> Are these already imported with the above? </p>
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.massdot.state.ma.us/planning/">massDOT Office of Planning</a> has quite a bit of data related to roads. See <a href="/wiki/MassDOT" title="MassDOT">massDOT</a> for more. </p>
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.mass.gov/anf/research-and-tech/it-serv-and-support/application-serv/office-of-geographic-information-massgis/datalayers/l3parcels.html">MassGIS Level 3 Assessors’ Parcel Mapping</a> has address information for buildings. </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Michigan">Michigan</span></h4> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://gis-michigan.opendata.arcgis.com/datasets/6319ec2d8bb445e990881c5fd9c4d198_0"><b>MDOT All Roads</b></a> consists of all roads from the Michigan Geographic Framework (MGF) base map. </p>
     <p><b>MDOT Bridge Connections</b> </p>
     <p>This <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://gis-michigan.opendata.arcgis.com/datasets/37c9d44bf04c446f992a79f7c2177b62%2039">page</a> provides information about the bridge connection layer which is an inventory of the bridge signs installed on MDOT bridges, railroad bridges and local bridges within Michigan Department of Transportation’s jurisdiction. </p>
     <p><b><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://gis-michigan.opendata.arcgis.com/datasets/ef46fd744ebf46cd966780ce1913e4db_37">MDOT Five Year Transportation Program</a></b> provides an annual document listing roads and bridge projects planned for the next five years. After being presented to the State Transportation Commission’s and gets its approval, the document is posted on MDOT’s Web site. </p>
     <p><b><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://gis-michigan.opendata.arcgis.com/datasets/6319ec2d8bb445e990881c5fd9c4d198_0">MDOT Lane Mile Inventory</a></b> </p>
     <p>This dataset consists of a GPS assisted windshield survey data collection of the number of lanes on any given segment of Michigan state highway. </p>
     <p><b><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://gis-michigan.opendata.arcgis.com/datasets/2dd7849806b6427b9aa30d284885b4f7_3">MDOT Mile Markers</a></b> has information about mile marker location along Michigan’s highways. The dataset includes descriptive information such as latitude and longitude, route name, region, TSC, county, control section number, physical reference(PR), number, PR mile point and mile number. </p>
     <p><b>Pavement Condition</b> </p>
     <p>SEMCOG(Southeast Michigan Council of Governments) open data provides <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://maps-semcog.opendata.arcgis.com/datasets/cc04b21f8bf545259dd97bfdef3d1f0c_0">road condition data</a> which is collected annually from late Spring to late Fall using RoadSoft. They also provide a dataset with roads extracted from version 16 of the Michigan Geographic Framework. The data can be downloaded from this <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://maps-semcog.opendata.arcgis.com/datasets/1292c9d3be1743009a8f0bf4b0a8de3b_0">page</a>. </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Detroit.2C_Michigan">Detroit, Michigan</span></h5> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://data.detroitmi.gov/Transportation/Traffic-Signals/dkav-a7rb">Traffic Signals</a> is a dataset with the location of all traffic signals in Detroit. </p>
     <p>The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://data.detroitmi.gov/Transportation/Traffic-Signs/nqdp-yans">page</a> contains the location of all traffic signs in Detroit. </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Minnesota">Minnesota</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Minnesota_Basemap_WMS_Services">Minnesota Basemap WMS Services</span></h5> 
     <p>MnGEO offers WMS services that are useful for basemap layers. The services include state-wide and metro imagery with resolutions of a meter or less. The services are available in geographic or UTM Zone15N spatial reference systems. More info at: <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://www.mngeo.state.mn.us/chouse/wms/wms_image_server_description.html">http://www.mngeo.state.mn.us/chouse/wms/wms_image_server_description.html</a> </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Minnesota_DOT_GIS_Data">Minnesota DOT GIS Data</span></h5> 
     <p>The Minnesota Department of Transportation releases 1:24000 scale GIS data files. From the site: "The data set includes information about transportation features (roads, railroads and navigable waters), as well as boundary information (State, County, and Municipal Boundaries, Mn/DOT District Boundaries, Civil, and Congressional Townships, State Forests and Parks, Military Reservations, Indian Reservation Lands, National Forests and Parks), and stream and lake locations." The files are "free of charge" from the MNDOT website: <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://www.dot.state.mn.us/maps/gisbase/html/datafiles.html">http://www.dot.state.mn.us/maps/gisbase/html/datafiles.html</a> but no mention of them being explicitly public domain/copyright free. It's probably worth contacting them though. --<a href="/wiki/User:BenFranske" title="User:BenFranske">BenFranske</a> 08:22, 18 June 2008 (UTC) </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="MetroGIS">MetroGIS</span></h5> 
     <p>The <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Council" title="Metropolitan Council">Metropolitan Council</a> publishes data in shapefile format here. The Metropolitan Council recently changed their metadata distribution language with the intention to be more accessible to uses such as importing into OpenStreetMap. </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Minnesota_DNR_Data_Deli_.28GIS_data.29">Minnesota DNR Data Deli (GIS data)</span></h5> 
     <p>The Minnesota Department of Natural Resources has a lot of Minnesota related GIS data. The information is accessible at the Minnesota Department of Resources Data Deli website: <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://deli.dnr.state.mn.us/index.html">http://deli.dnr.state.mn.us/index.html</a> It is typically provided in the form of shape files which can be converted to OSM or GPX files. This includes such data as: </p> 
     <ol>
      <li> Lakes, stream, rivers, wetlands</li> 
      <li> Roads, streets, forestry roads</li> 
      <li> Water access points, boat landings</li> 
      <li> State Snowmobile trails</li> 
      <li> State forests, parks, and WMA boundaries</li> 
      <li> State trails</li> 
      <li> State park trails</li> 
      <li> BWCA (Boundary Waters Canoe Area) boundary</li> 
      <li> State, federal, and county owned land</li> 
      <li> State forestry service administered land (different from official state forests)</li> 
      <li> Plus lot more and can be found here on the data download page: <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://deli.dnr.state.mn.us/data_search.html">http://deli.dnr.state.mn.us/data_search.html</a></li>
     </ol> 
     <p>This page: <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://deli.dnr.state.mn.us/about.html">http://deli.dnr.state.mn.us/about.html</a> contains general information about using the MN DNR data deli, contact information for the site, its data, and general questions. Also it has the official license, the Minnesota DNR GIS Data License Agreement, for this data which my reading would suggest that it could be added to OSM. </p> 
     <dl>
      <dd>
        According to my reading, Sections 1 and 6 of the DNR GIS Data License Agreement indicate that the data 
       <b>can not</b> be added to OSM under either the CC-SA-BY or the draft ODbL license. - I have attached a copy of the 
       <a href="/wiki/Talk:Potential_Datasources#Minnesota_Department_of_Natural_Resources_General_Geographic_Data_License_Agreement" title="Talk:Potential Datasources">MN DNR's GIS data license</a> to the Talk page --
       <a href="/wiki/User:DiverCTH" title="User:DiverCTH">DiverCTH</a> 00:08, 22 December 2009 (UTC)
      </dd>
     </dl> 
     <dl>
      <dd>
       <dl>
        <dd>
          Part 1 of the agreement says that if there is a dataset-specific license agreement distributed with the data, then that more specific agreement holds. Many of the datasets I've downloaded from the site have "None" for both "Access Constraints" and "Use Constraints". It seems like at least some of the data from the DNR Data Deli could be added to OSM. --
         <a href="/wiki/User:Stucki1" title="User:Stucki1">Stucki1</a> 31 December 2009
        </dd>
       </dl>
      </dd>
     </dl> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Mississippi">Mississippi</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="MARIS">MARIS</span></h5> 
     <p>Mississippi Automated Resource Information System (<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.maris.state.ms.us/home.htm">MARIS</a>) Technical Center website, providing access to Mississippi's statewide geographic information system (GIS). Through this site we offer you access to a range of resources, including: </p> 
     <ul>
      <li>search and retrieval of data descriptions (metadata)</li> 
      <li>retrieval of Mississippi data sets</li> 
      <li>posting of news related to GIS developments</li> 
      <li>announcements of upcoming meetings and events</li> 
      <li>mapping of data sets</li> 
      <li>access and retrieval to aerial photography covering Mississippi </li>
     </ul> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="MGC">MGC</span></h5> 
     <p>The Mississippi Geospatial Clearinghouse (<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.gis.ms.gov/Portal/">MGC</a>) provides access to a comprehensive spatial information warehouse of Geographic Information Systems (GIS) resources of Mississippi for use by government, academia, and the private sector. </p>
     <p>The Mississippi Geospatial Clearinghouse and MARIS are two separate entities. The Mississippi Geospatial Clearinghouse is assigned the responsibility of getting data to the public. Most of the data is government data that is considered "best available" data. MARIS provides MGC some data that MGC exposes on their behalf. </p>
     <p>Data in MGC has been confirmed public domain. (contact <a href="/wiki/User:Eladner" title="User:Eladner">Eladner</a> for details) </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Missouri">Missouri</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Missouri_Spatial_Data_Information_Service">Missouri Spatial Data Information Service</span></h5> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://msdis.missouri.edu/">MSDIS</a> is the public domain repository for the state of Missouri, housed by the University of Missouri at Columbia. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://msdis.missouri.edu/datasearch/ThemeList.jsp">Data layers</a> cover a wide range of resources compiled by state agencies, including natural resources, health services, and transportation networks. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://msdis.missouri.edu/maps/Connecting_to_Web_Mapping_Services.pdf">ArcIMS web services</a> are provided at <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://msdismapper.col.missouri.edu">http://msdismapper.col.missouri.edu</a>, including public domain leaf-off 2' pixel resolution aerial photography from 2007-2008. </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="St_Louis_County">St Louis County</span></h5> 
     <p>St Louis County Planning Department's <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.stlouisco.com/plan/gis/spatial_data.html">Data CD1</a> contains shapefiles as of July 2009 for political jurisdictions, service areas, schools, fire stations, landmarks, light rail lines and stations, street centerlines, and addressing. Missouri Law requires a county ordinance to place licensing and fee restrictions, which St Louis County does not have in place. </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Montana">Montana</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Montana_Cadastral_Data">Montana Cadastral Data</span></h5> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gis.mt.gov/">MAPP</a> is the site for Montana's Cadastral Data. </p>
     <p>Terms: This data is a cooperative effort between the Montana Department of Administration, (DOA) and the Montana Department of Revenue (DOR) other state agencies, local, governments, USDI BLM and private enterprise. The DOA provides mapped cadastral data, Web development, deployment, and enhancements. The DOR provides maintenance as well as CAMA data relating to the mapped cadastral data. Neither the DOA nor any associated partner, nor their employees, makes any warranty, expressed or implied, including the fitness for a particular purpose, or assumes any legal liability responsibility for the accuracy, completeness, or usefulness of any information, apparatus, product, or process disclosed, or represents that its use would not infringe privately owned rights. </p>
     <p>In layman's terms: the data not constitute a legal survey; inaccuracies exist with both the mapped data and the CAMA data; when seeking the definitive description of real property, consult the deed recorded at the local county courthouse. </p>
     <p>State law ( Montana Code Annotated 2-6-109 (1)(a) ) explicitly prohibits State agencies from selling or distributing a list of persons to be used as a mailing list without first securing the permission of those on the list. State law ( MCA 2-6-109 (1)(b) ) also explicitly prohibits anyone from using a list of persons prepared by a state agency as a mailing list without first securing the permission of those on the list. "A person violating the provisions of subsection (1)(b) is guilty of a misdemeanor." </p>
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gis.mt.gov/InfoHtm/parcelmeta.html#Distribution_Information">Distribution Metadata</a> </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Hampshire">New Hampshire</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Hampshire_DOT:_GIS_Data_Catalog">New Hampshire DOT: GIS Data Catalog</span></h5> 
     <p>It looks to be pretty comprehensive as far as transportation, with roads, bridges, rail. It also seems to include Town and County information as well as digital orthophotos. </p>
     <p>Note: Check all applicable copyrights on data before including. <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://www.nh.gov/dot/org/projectdevelopment/planning/gis/">http://www.nh.gov/dot/org/projectdevelopment/planning/gis/</a> </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Jersey">New Jersey</span></h4> 
     <p><i> Refer to the <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">New Jersey</a> project page for more information.</i> </p>
     <p>New Jersey 2007-2008 aerial photography are available online via WMS. There are no restrictions on its use. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://njgin.state.nj.us/NJ_NJGINExplorer/ShowMetadata.jsp?docId={DC1F4E29-28A5-11DB-9EFE-0003BA2C919E}">View metadata.</a> </p>
     <p>The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://njgin.state.nj.us">New Jersey Geographic Information Network</a> is the state's geospatial data clearinghouse. More GIS data freely available for download at <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.nj.gov/dep/gis/">NJDEP Bureau of GIS</a>. Always check the metadata for use restrictions. GIS data <b>maintained and published</b> by a state or local government entity is subject to <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://nj.gov/grc/public/">NJ's OPRA laws</a> and considered public domain. </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="New_Mexico">New Mexico</span></h4> 
     <p>The Pueblo of Acoma has offered license-free data it created as part of the federal "rural-addressing" project, which is designed to make it easier for emergency personnel to locate rural addresses. The data consists of a shapefile of road center lines on the reservation and adjoining areas. The tribal Director of Water and Wastewater, and the Director of Planning and Engineering both put in writing that the data is license-free. </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="New_York">New York</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Statewide">Statewide</span></h5> 
     <p>Parks and Trails New York has data for multi-use trails and park areas across the state. Discussions are underway with them about permission and licensing. </p>
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://www.ptny.org/">http://www.ptny.org/</a> </p>
     <p>The <b>New York State Dept. of Environmental Conservation (DEC)</b> has data for a number of features listed on the <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gis.ny.gov/gisdata/">NYS GIS Clearinghouse</a>'s <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gis.ny.gov/gisdata/inventories/member.cfm?OrganizationID=529">DEC page</a>. These include park and conservation area lands that have <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://lists.openstreetmap.org/pipermail/talk-us/2016-May/016290.html">already been</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://lists.openstreetmap.org/pipermail/talk-us/2016-September/016702.html">imported</a> into OSM, as well as <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gis.ny.gov/gisdata/inventories/details.cfm?DSID=1167">road/trails</a>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gis.ny.gov/gisdata/inventories/details.cfm?DSID=1258">points of interest</a> (campsites, parking, toilets, etc), and more. The metadata for these files indicates that <i>"1. Data may NOT be distributed outside DEC without permission by the Division of Lands and Forests, GIS Section. 2. The NYS DEC asks to be credited in derived products. 3. Secondary distribution of the data is not allowed."</i> From the talk-us mailing list it appears that permission has been <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://lists.openstreetmap.org/pipermail/talk-us/2016-May/016290.html">requested</a> and granted for at least a sub-set of this data. </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="New_York_City">New York City</span></h5> 
     <p>New York City Department of Information Technology and Telecommunications (DOITT) Map includes: building outlines, parks, green markets, schools, wifi hotspots, historic districts, landmarks, municipal boundaries, transportation details, and property info of all kinds. </p>
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://gis.nyc.gov/doitt/nycitymap/">http://gis.nyc.gov/doitt/nycitymap/</a> </p>
     <p>There is a feedback form for the map that might be used to initiate a request to share the info. </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="North_Carolina">North Carolina</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="North_Carolina_DOT:_GIS_data_including_Bikeroutes">North Carolina DOT: GIS data including Bikeroutes</span></h5> 
     <p>The NC Department of Transportation releases their bike routes as a GIS layer in <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ESRI" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ESRI">ESRI</a>. They may also have normal roads, but that's less of a point with <a href="/wiki/TIGER" title="TIGER">TIGER</a> available. </p> 
     <dl>
      <dd>
       NCDOT GIS Digital Bicycle Maps &amp; Route Information ? 
       <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://www.ncdot.org/it/gis/DataDistribution/BikeMaps/">http://www.ncdot.org/it/gis/DataDistribution/BikeMaps/</a> 
      </dd> 
      <dd>
       Google Cache (27 Feb 2010) ? 
       <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://74.125.93.132/search?sourceid=navclient-ff&amp;ie=UTF-8&amp;q=cache:http://www.ncdot.org/it/gis/DataDistribution/BikeMaps/">http://74.125.93.132/search?sourceid=navclient-ff&amp;ie=UTF-8&amp;q=cache:http://www.ncdot.org/it/gis/DataDistribution/BikeMaps/</a>
      </dd> 
      <dd>
       Wayback Cache (28 April 2006 forward) ? 
       <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://web.archive.org/web/*/http://www.ncdot.org/it/gis/DataDistribution/BikeMaps/">http://web.archive.org/web/*/http://www.ncdot.org/it/gis/DataDistribution/BikeMaps/</a>
      </dd>
     </dl> 
     <p>The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.nconemap.com/Default.aspx?tabid=286">NC OneMap ftp service description page</a> provides a list of files which can be downloaded and used "by anyone without restriction". However, meta-data associated with each file should be consulted to determine any <i>actual</i> restrictions on use and any attribution requirements. An e-mail from David Giordano at ncmail.net (listed contact) confirms this. The data is broadly broken down into two categories: vector data and raster (imagery) data. A WMS service has been purportedly set up. </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="NCSU_Library_North_Carolina_County_GIS_Data">NCSU Library North Carolina County GIS Data</span></h5> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="https://www.lib.ncsu.edu/gis/counties.html">https://www.lib.ncsu.edu/gis/counties.html</a> </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ohio">Ohio</span></h4> 
     <p>Central Ohio Transit Authority has public data for the following (bus routes, stops, park and rides, ammenities) available in shapefile format. Requests can be made at <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.cota.com/contact_cota.asp">[46]</a> </p>
     <p>OGRIP (Ohio Geographically Referenced Information Program) provides public data for road centerlines, aerial imagery, LIDAR, and much more. Mostly available in shapefile format. The main website <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://ogrip.oit.ohio.gov/">[47]</a> links to all of the data </p>
     <p>Ohio Metadata Explorer provides lots of public gis layers from different state and local departments. <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://metadataexplorer.gis.state.oh.us/metadataexplorer/explorer.jsp">[48]</a> </p>
     <p><br> NEO CANDO, (Northeast Ohio Community and Neighborhood Data for Organizing) contains information on properties within the City of Cleveland. License status is currently unknown. <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://neocando.case.edu">[49]</a> </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Oklahoma">Oklahoma</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Murray_County">Murray County</span></h5> 
     <p>See <a href="/wiki/Oklahoma/Import/Murray" title="Oklahoma/Import/Murray"> import page</a> </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Oregon">Oregon</span></h4> 
     <p>Refer to the more detailed <a href="/wiki/Oregon" title="Oregon">Oregon</a> page. </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pennsylvania">Pennsylvania</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Allegheny_County.2C_Pa">Allegheny County, Pa</span></h5> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.alleghenycounty.us/dcs/gis.aspx">Allegheny County</a> has very nice, accurate GIS data available in both shapefiles and as WMS layers at <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.pasda.psu.edu/">PASDA</a>. These are much more accurate then the TIGER lines, and include bike paths and pedestrian-only ways. </p>
     <p>I've spoken to them on the phone (on 7-8-2008), and they consider this data to be in the Public Domain. I'm trying to figure out how to upload this data to OSM - if anyone had tips, I'd love to have them. --<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Morgan-pgh&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Morgan-pgh (page does not exist)">Morgan-pgh</a> 16:39, 10 July 2008 (UTC) </p>
     <p>Here are some old discussions on the topic of importing these data sets: <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://lists.openstreetmap.org/pipermail/talk-us/2008-July/000238.html">[50]</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://lists.openstreetmap.org/pipermail/talk-us/2014-February/012668.html">[51]</a> <a href="/wiki/User:Abbafei" title="User:Abbafei">Abbafei</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Abbafei" title="User talk:Abbafei">talk</a>) 05:10, 27 April 2014 (UTC) </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Philadelphia">Philadelphia</span></h5> 
     <p>GIS data is also abundant for Philly at <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.pasda.psu.edu/">PASDA</a>. (click "Download Data" and search for keyword "Philadelphia".) Useful shapefiles include bike network, building footprints, parks, schools, fire stations, and railroads. Presumably the shapefiles that originate from the City of Philadelphia are in the public domain as it is a government entity. </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Pittsburgh">Pittsburgh</span></h5> 
     <p>The City of Pittsburgh is currently adopting an <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://pittsburghpa.gov/district4/open-data">open data program</a>. They have lots of interesting <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://pittsburghpa.gov/dcp/gis/gis-data">data</a>! Note that they have an OSM <a class="external text" href="https://www.openstreetmap.org/user/Pittsburgh%20City%20Planning">account</a>. <a href="/wiki/User:Abbafei" title="User:Abbafei">Abbafei</a> (<a href="/wiki/User_talk:Abbafei" title="User talk:Abbafei">talk</a>) 05:10, 27 April 2014 (UTC) </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Rhode_Island">Rhode Island</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Statewide_2">Statewide</span></h5> 
     <p>The Rhode Island Geographic Information System (RIGIS) Consortium recently made their expansive <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.edc.uri.edu/rigis/data/">data catalog</a> openly available as of September 1st of 2014. All data is available in shapefiles, though some of the URLs to SHP versions are currently dead. The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.edc.uri.edu/rigis/distributionPolicy.html">Data Distribution Policy</a> states: </p>
     <p><i>"All data distributed by RIGIS are provided 'as is.' The producer(s) of these data, contributors to these data, the Rhode Island Geographic Information System (RIGIS) consortium, the State of Rhode Island, and the University of Rhode Island do not make any warranties of any kind for these data, and are not liable for any loss or damage however and whenever caused by any use of these data. Please acknowledge both RIGIS and the primary producer(s) of these data in any derived products. Versions of the RIGIS logo suitable for both printed and web-based products are available at <a rel="nofollow" class="external free" href="http://www.edc.uri.edu/rigis/logos">http://www.edc.uri.edu/rigis/logos</a>".</i> </p>
     <p>Therefore, <b>all data from their catalogs needs to have <tt style="background:#EEF" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><bdi style="white-space:nowrap"><a href="/wiki/Key:source" title="Key:source">source</a></bdi>=<a href="/w/index.php?title=Tag:source%3DRIGIS&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Tag:source=RIGIS (page does not exist)"><bdi>RIGIS</bdi></a></tt> on it.</b> Note that the metadata for the datasets still might include copies of the former license, even though it has been superseded; this is no cause for concern. </p>
     <p><br> </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tennessee">Tennessee</span></h4> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.state.tn.us/environment/parks/gis/data/">Tennessee State Parks</a> </p>
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://tnmap.state.tn.us/portal/">State GIS portal</a> but no direct downloads. </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Texas">Texas</span></h4> 
     <p>Texas provides some good data from the Texas Natural Resources Information System (<a href="/wiki/TNRIS" title="TNRIS">TNRIS</a>) <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.tnris.org">[52]</a>. <del>I can't tell if the data's completely PD, or how accurate it is yet,</del> but I work with this data, and it seems pretty close for what I use it for. </p> 
     <dl>
      <dd>
       Update: Just received email from TNRIS. Their data is public domain. From the email:"If you can credit us, that would be great."
       <a href="/wiki/User:25or6to4" title="User:25or6to4">25or6to4</a> 18:37, 8 July 2009 (UTC)
      </dd>
     </dl> 
     <p>Texas Parks and Wildlife <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.tpwd.state.tx.us/landwater/land/maps/gis/data_downloads/">Statewide GIS data</a> --<a href="/wiki/User:Dalep" title="User:Dalep">Dalep</a> 01:29, 1 September 2008 (UTC) </p>
     <p>The City of Austin has an excellent set of GIS data available for download as shapefiles covering the city and its environs. Not only are there up-to-date layers for streets and arterials, but also water features, railroads, political boundaries, etc. There also is a comprehensive file of property parcels, and another file of points for discrete addresses. The data is stated as being in the public domain on the map request form: "GIS data sets are in the public domain and may be copied without permission, though citation of the source is appreciated." <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="ftp://ftp.ci.austin.tx.us/GIS-Data/Regional/coa_gis.html">[53]</a> </p>
     <p>The City of Frisco has an excellent set of GIS data available for download as shapefiles <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.friscotexas.gov/departments/gis/Pages/GISData.aspx">[54]</a> covering the city and its environs. There is Transportation, Points of Interest, Land Records, Municipal Boundaries, Zoning and Other Districts, and Monumentation. An *official from the GIS department sent this email to Martijn van Excel (Date: Mon, Feb 2, 2015 at 3:22 PM -0800): "We’d be happy for you to use our data in updating the Open Street Map database. We post our data as public information without a particular license, although we do include a readme file which includes a disclaimer with our data downloads. I don’t believe that any particular disclaimer or attribution would be required in OSM after using our data in order to update your database. Frisco GIS official: John Morley,GIS Coordinator,City of Frisco,972.292.5173,jmorley@friscotexas.gov </p>
     <p>The City of Dallas has a number of GIS resources available for download <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://gis.dallascityhall.com/shapezip.htm">[55]</a>, including building footprints, parks and trails, and hydrologic features. After contacting the City's GIS department about usage, I received the following response: <i>"We provide the data without restriction or guarantees of fitness for any purposes. We don't have any authority to grant or recognize the use of the data for any particular purpose(s). We consider it to fall under the heading of "public information", so it is available to use as you see fit. Perhaps you might use the Texas Public Information Act for your citation. Once you download the data, it is yours and we assume no responsibility or liability. Per State Law, we fully disclaim its use for any and all purposes.</i> <i>Regards, Michael R Miller, GIS Technical Manager, Communications &amp; Information Services, Innovation &amp; Information Management Services, City GIS Services, Michael.Miller2@DallasCityHall.com, 214.670.0876" </i> -<a href="/wiki/User:Andrew_Matheny" title="User:Andrew Matheny">Andrew Matheny</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:Andrew_Matheny&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:Andrew Matheny (page does not exist)">talk</a>) 16:20, 29 December 2016 (UTC) </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Utah">Utah</span></h4> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://gis.utah.gov/data/aerial-photography/">Utah GIS portal</a> "The State Geographic Information Database (SGID) contains files and links to several different categories of data sets. Data presented for download on this site is considered to be in the <b>public domain</b>." </p>
     <p>Some data sets have required disclaimers and attribution for printed and direct use. </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Vermont">Vermont</span></h4> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://geodata.vermont.gov/">Vermont Center for Geographic Information (VGCI)</a> - The <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://vcgi.vermont.gov/sites/vcgi/files/warehouse/VCGI_Warranty_Copyright_Notice_2013.pdf">Warranty &amp; Copyright notice</a> mentions only that <i>non-value added</i> sale is prohibited: </p> 
     <blockquote>
      "4.1 For all products, services, Internet Website, and data the direct, non-value added, reproduction of State of Vermont or VCGI’s products, services, Website, or data with intent to sell and without the written consent of VCGI."
     </blockquote> 
     <p>In response to a request for clarification, the following statement was received from John E. Adams AICP, Director of the Vermont Center for Geographic Information. <i>(<a href="/w/index.php?title=User:Adamfranco&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User:Adamfranco (page does not exist)">Adamfranco</a> (<a href="/w/index.php?title=User_talk:Adamfranco&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="User talk:Adamfranco (page does not exist)">talk</a>) 14:52, 21 September 2017 (UTC))</i> </p> 
     <blockquote>
      "The State of Vermont Center for Geographic Information has no objections to geodata derived in part from data-sets published by the Vermont Center for Geographic Information in the Vermont Open Geodata Portal being incorporated into the OpenStreetMap project geodata database and released under a free and open license."
     </blockquote> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Virginia">Virginia</span></h4> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Statewide_3">Statewide</span></h5> 
     <p>See the <a href="/wiki/Virginia#Resources" title="Virginia">Virginia page</a> for resources. </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Town_of_Blacksburg">Town of Blacksburg</span></h5> 
     <ul>
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.gis.lib.vt.edu/gis_data/Blacksburg/GISPage">Blacksburg GIS Data Distribution Site</a></li>
     </ul> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Montgomery_County">Montgomery County</span></h5> 
     <ul>
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.lib.vt.edu/subjects/maps/montgomery_gis.html">Montgomery County GIS data layers</a></li>
     </ul> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Washington">Washington</span></h4> 
     <p>
      <strike>
       links to various 
       <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.leaseown.org/Resources/WA_maps_data.html">Washington agencies</a>
      </strike> (out dated) </p> 
     <ul>
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.blm.gov/or/gis/data.php">US Bureau of Land Mangagement Oregon/WA</a></li> 
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.dahp.wa.gov/pages/EnvironmentalReview/GIS.htm">Washington Department of Archaeology and Historic Preservation</a> (Much of the DAHP data is not available due to looting issues, however historic places may be possible to obtain)</li> 
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://ww4.doh.wa.gov/gis/gisdata.htm">Washington State Department of Health</a></li> 
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.ecy.wa.gov/services/gis/data/data.htm">Washington Department of Ecology GIS</a></li> 
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.wsdot.wa.gov/Mapsdata/geodatacatalog/">Washington Department of Transportation GeoData Distribution Catalog</a></li> 
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.dnr.wa.gov/BusinessPermits/Topics/Data/Pages/gis_data_center.aspx">Washington Department of Natural Resources</a>(<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.dnr.wa.gov/Publications/itd_see_license_agreement.pdf">Requires permission for derivitave work which has not been obtained</a>)</li> 
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://wa-node.gis.washington.edu/">University of Washington Geospatial Clearinghouse</a> (The Washington Geospatial clearinghouse contains data from many different sources with different licenses)</li> 
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://wagic.wa.gov/">Washington State Geographic Information Council</a></li>
     </ul> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Bellingham.2C_WA">Bellingham, WA</span></h5> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.cob.org/services/maps/gis/">Bellingham's GIS department</a> has given consent for their data to be used in OSM and redistributed under the ODbL. A copy of correspondence with them can be found on <a href="/wiki/User:Dericke" title="User:Dericke">Dericke</a>'s user page. <a href="/wiki/Bellingham,_Washington" title="Bellingham, Washington"> Bellingham on OSM</a> </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Clallam_County.2C_WA">Clallam County, WA</span></h5> 
     <ul>
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://science.nature.nps.gov/nrdata/quickoutput.cfm?statecode=wa&amp;Parkcode=olym">Olympic National Park</a></li> 
      <li> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.fs.fed.us/r6/data-library/gis/olympic/">Olympic National Forest</a></li>
     </ul> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Clark_County.2C_WA">Clark County, WA</span></h5> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gis.clark.wa.gov/gishome/">Clark County GIS</a> </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Spokane.2C_WA">Spokane, WA</span></h5> 
     <p>The city of Spokane, WA publishes free (gratis) <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.spokanecity.org/services/gis/data/">GIS datasets</a> for street centerlines, parks, waterways, city boundaries, etc. The centerlines seem to cover all of Spokane County. </p>
     <p>Their data is of much better quality than the TIGER/Line data—though TIGER/Line does cover a few things that Spokane's data does not: roads in some trailer park in the Latah area (Club Dr., etc. around <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://openstreetmap.org/?lat=47.63783&amp;lon=-117.44589&amp;zoom=16&amp;layers=B0FT">47.63783,-117.44589</a>); Centennial Trail (partial coverage). </p>
     <p>I'm contacting them to see if we can include this in OSM. --<a href="/wiki/User:Jpl" title="User:Jpl">Jpl</a> 01:29, 15 March 2008 (UTC) </p> 
     <h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Whatcom_County.2C_WA">Whatcom County, WA</span></h5> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://wagic.wa.gov/Metadata/Whatcom/wagicwha.htm">Whatcom County GIS</a> They need to be contacted regarding use </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="West_Virgina">West Virgina</span></h4> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://wvgis.wvu.edu//data/data.php?action=search&amp;subject=ALL+SUBJECTS&amp;location=ALL+LOCATIONS&amp;fulllist=1&amp;list=1">West Virginia GIS Data Clearinghouse</a> </p> 
     <h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wisconsin">Wisconsin</span></h4> 
     <p><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.wisconsinview.org/">WisconsinView</a> announced their aerial and satellite imagery is now available under <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://wiki.creativecommons.org/CC0">CC0</a> </p>

    <div class="portal" role="navigation" id="p-tb" aria-labelledby="p-tb-label"> 
     <h3 id="p-tb-label">Tools</h3> 
     <div class="body">
